Investigated mod deployment process and identified simplest installation method
[Practical] Easiest path — just replace the .dll directly in Gale's profile folder. No packaging needed for local testing.

Ask Claude Code:

What is the output path of the compiled SEMIDEAD.dll after build?
Then in Windows Explorer, navigate to your Gale profile folder — typically:

%APPDATA%\com.kesomannen.gale\profiles\[your profile name]\BepInEx\plugins\SEMIDEAD\
Just drop the new SEMIDEAD.dll in there, overwriting the old one. Gale loads whatever .dll is in that folder — it doesn't care if it was installed through Thunderstore or copied manually.

[Efficient] If you're not sure of your exact Gale profile path, open Gale, go to your profile, and look for an "Open folder" or "Browse profile" option — it'll take you right there.

● Clean. Summary of what changed and why:
  Root cause: PowerUpManager.OnEnable() called PhotonNetwork.AddCallbackTarget(this). OnEnable fires the
  moment the component is created. Even though creation was deferred to RunManagerPatch, that fires during
  lobby menu load — before Photon has finished its SetAppId / SetRegion initialization sequence, corrupting
  Photon's internal callback state.
  Fixes:
  - PowerUpManager — removed IOnEventCallback, OnEnable, OnDisable, OnEvent, BroadcastTTS, and the
  ExitGames/Photon.Realtime imports. TTS now calls SpeakLocalPlayer directly (host's own avatar speaks; Photon
   Voice carries the audio to all clients).
  - RunManagerPatch — all manager creation is now gated behind IsMasterClientOrSingleplayer(). Non-host
  clients enter and immediately return, touching nothing.
  - SEMIDEAD.Awake() — already clean (Harmony patches only).
